	<script type="text/javascript" language="JavaScript">
	$(document).ready(function() {
		$('#btn_search').click(searchcourses);
		$('#frm_schedule').submit(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			searchcourses();
		});
	});

	function searchcourses() {
		var coursenumber = $.trim($('#txt_coursenumber').val());
		var alphanumeric_pattern = /^[a-zA-Z0-9\s\.\-]+$/;

		if(coursenumber != '') {
			if( ! alphanumeric_pattern.test(coursenumber)) {
				alert('Course number must be alphanumeric.');
			} else {
				window.location = 'https://crs.upd.edu.ph/course_catalog/index/' + coursenumber;
			}
		}

	}

	</script>

This would also cover the interplay of financial institutions (e.g., commercial banks, investment banks, insurance companies, etc.) and an overview of their asset-liability management, and the factors that influence the development of institutional structure and degree of specialization. </td>

		<td>Derivatives securities like features, options and swaps, their underlying theories and principles, their basic characteristics. Includes the basic principles, and strategies in using these derivative securities for risk management. It will likewise cover an introduction to disintermediation and securitization/financial engineering. </td>
		<td><abbr title="Department of Accounting and Finance" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted;">DAF</abbr></td>
	</tr>
		<tr class="tr_odd">
		<td>MSFIN 227</td>
		<td>International Finance</td>
		<td>Covers the complexities of doing business in more than one currency. Includes an overview of international financial markets, exchange rate systems and theories of exchange rate behavior. Special focus is on exchange rate risk management through hedging in the foreign exchange markets and money markets. The course will also cover trade financing instruments and risk management. </td>
		<td><abbr title="Department of Accounting and Finance" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted;">DAF</abbr></td>
	</tr>
		<tr class="tr_even">
		<td>MSFIN 228</td>
		<td>Management of Commercial Banks</td>
		<td>This course covers an in-depth study of asset-liability management of commercial banks and management accounting and control for financial institutions. Also included are basic principles and practices of credit, involving credit policy formulation, credit evaluation (initiation, analysis, packaging, and approval), credit monitoring, remedial management and liquidation, and treasury management covering basic strategies of managing the funding sources of financial intermediaries, and the management of the liquidity position. </td>
		<td><abbr title="Department of Accounting and Finance" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted;">DAF</abbr></td>

		<tr class="tr_even">
		<td>MuPC 11</td>
		<td>Piano Minor Class 1</td>
		<td>This course is being proposed to address the needs of students who have no knowledge of piano playing. Students will be grouped together in small groups to receive an hour of instruction.  This will allow more topics to be covered, such as sight reading, transposition, harmonization, keyboard harmony, improvisation and ensemble playing.  However, MuP 11 (individual lessons) will still be retained for students who already know how to play the instrument.  Therefore, MuPC 11 may be a substitute course for MuP 11.</td>
		<td><abbr title="Department of Keyboard" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted;">DKey</abbr></td>
	</tr>
		<tr class="tr_odd">
		<td>MuPC 21</td>
		<td>Piano Minor Class 2</td>
		<td>This course is a continuation of MuPC 11.  It will reinforce and upgrade the skills acquired in MuPC 11.  MuP 21 will still be retained for students who are more adept at piano playing.  Thus, MuPC 21 may be a substitute course for MuP 21.</td>
		<td><abbr title="Department of Keyboard" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted;">DKey</abbr></td>
	</tr>
		<tr class="tr_even">

<script type="text/javascript">
			
		$(document).ready(function() {
			
			//set the width per footer_expander element
			var expander_count = $('.footerlink').length;
			var expander_width = (83/expander_count);
			
			var i = 0;
			$.each($(".footerlink"), function(index, value){
				$(this).css('width', expander_width+'%');
				$(this).css('left', (((expander_width)*i)+10)+'%');
				i++;
			});
			
			$(".footerlink,.footer_expander").hover(
				function(){
					$(this).animate({ height: "30"}, 50);
				},
				function(){
					$(this).animate({ height: "16"}, 50);
				
				}
			);
			
			//set the width per footer_expander element
			var division_count = $('.footer_division').length;
			var division_width = (88/division_count);
			division_width = division_width+'%';
			
			$.each($(".footer_division"), function(index, value){
				$(this).css('width', division_width);
			});
			
		function change_acadtermtype() {
			return document.location = 'https://crs.upd.edu.ph/user/switch_acadtermtype/' + $(this).val();
		}

		function change_role() {
			return document.location = 'https://crs.upd.edu.ph/user/switch_role/' + $(this).val();
		}

		function show_roles() {
			$("#span_role").addClass("hidden");
			$("#span_role-choices").removeClass("hidden");
		}

		function show_acadtermtypes() {
			$("#span_acadtermtype").addClass("hidden");
			$("#span_acadtermtype-choices").removeClass("hidden");
		}

	 });
	 
	
	function showFooter(){
		$('#footer').slideDown(150);
		$('.footermin').hide();
	}
	function hideFooter(){
		$('#footer').slideUp(150);
		$('.footermin').show();
	}
	</script>
